   # âœ… BÆ°á»›c 1: GÃ³i toÃ n bá»™ ná»™i dung trong `<App>` vÃ o 1 `div` cÃ³ class Ä‘á»™ng:

> ğŸ”¹ `transition  transform`: mÆ°á»£t.

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer  motion'


export default function Navbar() {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false)
  const [showHeader, setShowHeader] = useState(false)


  useEffect(() => {
    const handleScroll = () => {
      const scrollY = window.scrollY
      if (scrollY > 1) setShowHeader(true)
    }


    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
    return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
  }, [])


  return (
    <motion.header
      initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
      animate={{ opacity: showHeader ? 1 : 0 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.3, ease: 'easeOut' }}
      className={`
        fixed top  0 left  0 z  50 w  full
        transition  all duration  1000 ease  in  out xl:pt  5
        ${showHeader ? 'pointer  events  auto bg  black/40  shadow  md border  b border  white/10' : 'pointer  events  none'}
      `}
    >

 <div
     
        className={`flex justify  between items  center px  4 pt  2 xl:px  16 xl:pt  4 pb  2 h  16
        ${showHeader ? 'pt  [50px] pb  6' : 'pt  0'}
      `}>
        <img src="/logo.png" className="object  cover w  20 xl:w  22" />


        {/* Mobile Button */}
        <button
          className="z  50 w  10 h  10 relative xl:hidden"
          onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
        >
          <span className={`absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? 'rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          <span className={`absolute top  [16px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  opacity duration  300 ${isOpen ? 'opacity  0   translate  x  1/2' : 'opacity  100   translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          <span className={`absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? '  rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
        </button>


        {/* Desktop Menu */}
        <nav className="hidden xl:flex space  x  8 text  white font  semibold">
          <div className="relative group">
            <motion.a whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }} transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300 }} className="cursor  pointer hover:font  bold">About</motion.a>
            <div className="h  full">
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg
                opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0
                transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500
              ">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">History</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Vision</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Leadership</a>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>


          <div className="relative group">
            <span className="cursor  pointer">Residences</span>
            <div className="h  full">
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg
                opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0
                transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500
              ">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Floor</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Plans</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Gallery</a>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>


          <a href="#location" className="hover:text  amber  300">Location</a>
          <a href="https://masterisehomes.com/lien  he" className="hover:text  amber  300">Contact</a>
        </nav>
      </div>


      {/* Mobile Sidebar */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {isOpen && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ x: '100%' }}
            animate={{ x: 0 }}
            exit={{ x: '100%' }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.5, ease: 'easeInOut' }}
            className="fixed top  0 right  0 h  full w  72 bg  gray  700 text  white p  6 shadow  lg space  y  4 opacity  [.90] xl:hidden"
          >
            <h1 className="text  2xl font  bold mb  6 mt  16">Menu</h1>
            <div className="space  y  6">
              <div>
                <p className="font  bold">About</p>
                <ul className="pl  3 pt  2 text  sm text  gray  300 space  y  1">
                  <li>History</li>
                  <li>Vision</li>
                  <li>Leadership</li>
                </ul>
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="font  bold">Residences</p>
                <ul className="pl  3 pt  2 text  sm text  gray  300 space  y  1">
                  <li>Floor Plans</li>
                  <li>Amenities</li>
                  <li>Gallery</li>
                </ul>
              </div>
              <a className="block font  bold">Location</a>
              <a className="block font  bold">Contact</a>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>

     
    </motion.header>
  )
}

```jsx
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
```
import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer  motion'


export default function Navbar({ onSidebarToggle }) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false)
  const [showHeader, setShowHeader] = useState(false)

   // Gá»­i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i sidebar cho App má»—i khi thay Ä‘á»•i
  useEffect(() => {
    onSidebarToggle?.(isOpen)
  }, [isOpen, onSidebarToggle])



  useEffect(() => {
    const handleScroll = () => {
      const scrollY = window.scrollY
      if (scrollY > 1) setShowHeader(true)
    }


    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
    return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
  }, [])


  return (
    <motion.header
      initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
      animate={{ opacity: showHeader ? 1 : 0 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.3, ease: 'easeOut' }}
      className={`
        fixed top  0 left  0 z  50 w  full
        transition  all duration  1000 ease  in  out xl:pt  5
        ${showHeader ? 'pointer  events  auto bg  black/40  shadow  md border  b border  white/10' : 'pointer  events  none'}
      `}
    >

 <div
     
        className={`flex justify  between items  center px  4 pt  2 xl:px  16 xl:pt  4 pb  2 h  16
        ${showHeader ? 'pt  [50px] pb  6' : 'pt  0'}
      `}>
        <img src="/logo.png" className="object  cover w  20 xl:w  22" />


        {/* Mobile Button */}
        <button
          className="z  50 w  10 h  10 relative xl:hidden"
          onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)

          }
        >
          <span className={`absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? 'rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          <span className={`absolute top  [16px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  opacity duration  300 ${isOpen ? 'opacity  0   translate  x  1/2' : 'opacity  100   translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          <span className={`absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? '  rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
        </button>


        {/* Desktop Menu */}
        <nav className="hidden xl:flex space  x  8 text  white font  semibold">
          <div className="relative group">
            <motion.a whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }} transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300 }} className="cursor  pointer hover:font  bold">About</motion.a>
            <div className="h  full">

                opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0
                transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500
              ">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">History</a>

Cáº£m Æ¡n chiáº¿n há»¯u Ä‘Ã£ gá»­i ká»¹ cáº£ `Navbar` vÃ  `App.jsx`, lá»—i **scroll bá»‹ Ä‘á»©ng cá»©ng luÃ´n khi má»Ÿ sidebar mobile** lÃ  do:

> âœ… `document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'` ngáº¯t toÃ n bá»™ scroll **cá»§a `body`**, nhÆ°ng ná»™i dung cuá»™n hiá»‡n táº¡i náº±m **trong `main`**.  
> VÃ¬ tháº¿ nÃ³ khÃ³a sai chá»—, khiáº¿n scroll Ä‘á»©ng cá»©ng toÃ n bá»™!

  

## âœ… CÃ¡ch sá»­a Ä‘Ãºng vÃ  mÆ°á»£t:

    âœ… **CÃ¡ch 1 (khuyÃªn dÃ¹ng)**: DÃ¹ng Tailwind + `class` Ä‘á»ƒ "khÃ³a" cuá»™n Ä‘Ãºng má»¥c tiÃªu

    ğŸ‘‰ BÆ°á»›c 1: Trong `App.jsx`, thÃªm logic toggle class `overflow  hidden` vÃ o `main`

Thay:

```jsx
<main className={`relative w  full min  h  screen transition  transform duration  600 ease  in  out xl:pt  0 ${
  sidebarOpen ? '  translate  x  [200px] bg  black' : ''
}`}>
```

ğŸ‘‰ Báº±ng:

```jsx
<main className={`relative w  full min  h  screen transition  transform duration  600 ease  in  out xl:pt  0 ${
  sidebarOpen ? '  translate  x  [200px] bg  black overflow  hidden h  screen' : ''
}`}>
```

> âœ… ThÃªm `overflow  hidden h  screen` chá»‰ khi `sidebarOpen === true`, cÃ²n láº¡i cuá»™n bÃ¬nh thÆ°á»ng.

  

    âœ… **BÆ°á»›c 2: XoÃ¡ Ä‘oáº¡n `document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'` trong `Navbar`**

```jsx
useEffect(() => {
  if (isOpen) {
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'
  } else {
    document.body.style.overflow = 'auto'
  }
}, [isOpen])
```

ğŸ‘‰ **XÃ“A Ä‘oáº¡n nÃ y Ä‘i** vÃ¬ ta Ä‘Ã£ xá»­ lÃ½ scroll báº±ng class Tailwind trong `App.jsx`.

  

## âœ… Hoáº·c cÃ¡ch 2: Náº¿u váº«n muá»‘n kiá»ƒm soÃ¡t `body`, thÃ¬ pháº£i `setTimeout`

```jsx
useEffect(() => {
  setTimeout(() => {
    document.body.style.overflow = isOpen ? 'hidden' : 'auto'
  }, 50)
}, [isOpen])
```

> NhÆ°ng cÃ¡ch nÃ y dá»… bug khi scroll target khÃ´ng náº±m á»Ÿ `body`. NÃªn **khuyÃªn dÃ¹ng cÃ¡ch 1**.

  

## âœ… Tá»•ng káº¿t:

   âŒ KhÃ´ng nÃªn `document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'` náº¿u scroll khÃ´ng náº±m á»Ÿ body.
   âœ… Tá»‘t nháº¥t toggle `overflow  hidden h  screen` á»Ÿ `<main>` náº¿u dÃ¹ng Tailwind + sidebar slide.
   âœ… CÃ¡ch nÃ y khÃ´ng cháº·n scroll trÃªn desktop, mÃ  chá»‰ khi má»Ÿ sidebar mobile thÃ´i.

  

Chiáº¿n há»¯u fix theo lÃ  á»•n ngay. Náº¿u sidebar má»Ÿ mÃ  muá»‘n **scroll ná»™i dung trong sidebar váº«n Ä‘Æ°á»£c**, thÃ¬ mÃ¬nh set `overflow  y  auto` cho `motion.div` sidebar ná»¯a lÃ  hoÃ n chá»‰nh.

LÃ m xong test láº¡i, cÃ³ gÃ¬ nháº¯n tao fix tiáº¿p âœŠ
user
chiáº¿n há»¯u cÃ³ 2 váº«n Ä‘á», khoÃ¡ nÃ³ mÃ  ko lÆ°á»›t á»Ÿ trong Ä‘Æ°á»£c, mÃ  khi má»Ÿ ra nÃ³ váº«n vá» Ä‘áº§u trang, cÃ³ cÃ¡ch nÃ o Ä‘ang lÆ°á»›t mÃ  xem á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã³ ko, chÆ°a ká»ƒ t muá»‘n lÃ  khi má»Ÿ sidebar máº¥y cÃ¡i chá»¯ cá»§a nÃ³ náº±m qua háº¿t bÃªn trÃ¡i rá»•i ko tháº¥y gÃ¬ háº¿t ngoáº¡i trá»« dáº¥u X 

Ä‘Ã¢y lÃ  file Navbar nÃ¨ chiáº¿n há»¯u 

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer  motion'


export default function Navbar({ onSidebarToggle }) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false)
  const [showHeader, setShowHeader] = useState(false)

   // Gá»­i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i sidebar cho App má»—i khi thay Ä‘á»•i
  useEffect(() => {
    onSidebarToggle?.(isOpen)
  }, [isOpen, onSidebarToggle])



  useEffect(() => {
    const handleScroll = () => {
      const scrollY = window.scrollY
      if (scrollY > 1) setShowHeader(true)
    }


    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
    return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
  }, [])

 







  return (
    <motion.header
      initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
      animate={{ opacity: showHeader ? 1 : 0 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.3, ease: 'easeOut' }}
      className={`
        fixed top  0 left  0 z  50 w  full
        transition  all duration  1000 ease  in  out xl:pt  5
        ${showHeader ? 'pointer  events  auto bg  black/40  shadow  md border  b border  white/10' : 'pointer  events  none'}
      `}
    >

 <div
     
        className={`flex justify  between items  center px  4 pt  2 xl:px  16 xl:pt  4 pb  2 h  16
        ${showHeader ? 'pt  [50px] pb  6' : 'pt  0'}
      `}>
        <img src="/logo.png" className="object  cover w  20 xl:w  22" />


        {/* Mobile Button */}
        <button
          className="z  50 w  10 h  10 relative xl:hidden"
          onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)

          }
        >
          <span className={`absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? 'rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          <span className={`absolute top  [16px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  opacity duration  300 ${isOpen ? 'opacity  0   translate  x  1/2' : 'opacity  100   translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          <span className={`absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? '  rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer  motion'


export default function Navbar({ onSidebarToggle }) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false)
  const [showHeader, setShowHeader] = useState(false)

   // Gá»­i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i sidebar cho App má»—i khi thay Ä‘á»•i
  useEffect(() => {
    onSidebarToggle?.(isOpen)
  }, [isOpen, onSidebarToggle])



  useEffect(() => {
    const handleScroll = () => {
      const scrollY = window.scrollY
      if (scrollY > 1) setShowHeader(true)
    }


    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
    return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
  }, [])

 







  return (
    <motion.header
      initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
      animate={{ opacity: showHeader ? 1 : 0 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.3, ease: 'easeOut' }}
      className={`
        fixed top  0 left  0 z  50 w  full
        transition  all duration  1000 ease  in  out xl:pt  5
        ${showHeader ? 'pointer  events  auto bg  black/40  shadow  md border  b border  white/10' : 'pointer  events  none'}
      `}
    >

 <div
     
        className={`flex justify  between items  center px  4 pt  2 xl:px  16 xl:pt  4 pb  2 h  16
        ${showHeader ? 'pt  [50px] pb  6' : 'pt  0'}
      `}>
        <img src="/logo.png" className="object  cover w  20 xl:w  22" />


        {/* Mobile Button */}
        <button
          className="z  50 w  10 h  10 relative xl:hidden"
          onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)

          }
        >
          <span className={`absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? 'rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          <span className={`absolute top  [16px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  opacity duration  300 ${isOpen ? 'opacity  0   translate  x  1/2' : 'opacity  100   translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          <span className={`absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? '  rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
        </button>


        {/* Desktop Menu */}
        <nav className="hidden xl:flex space  x  8 text  white font  semibold">
          <div className="relative group">
            <motion.a whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }} transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300 }} className="cursor  pointer hover:font  bold">About</motion.a>
            <div className="h  full">
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg
                opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0
                transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500
              ">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">History</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Vision</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Leadership</a>
              </div>
            </div>

import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer  motion'


export default function Navbar({ onSidebarToggle }) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false)
  const [showHeader, setShowHeader] = useState(false)

   // Gá»­i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i sidebar cho App má»—i khi thay Ä‘á»•i
  useEffect(() => {
    onSidebarToggle?.(isOpen)
  }, [isOpen, onSidebarToggle])



useEffect(() => {
  const handleScroll = () => {
    const scrollY = window.scrollY
    setShowHeader(scrollY > 1)
    setIsTop(scrollY <= 1)
  }


  window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
  return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
}, [])



 


const [isTop, setIsTop] = useState(true)







  return (
    <main>
 <motion.header
      initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
      animate={{ opacity: showHeader ? 1 : 0 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.3, ease: 'easeOut' }}
      className={`
        fixed top  0 left  0 z  10 w  full
        transition  all duration  1000 ease  in  out xl:pt  5
        ${showHeader ? 'pointer  events  auto bg  black/40  shadow  md border  b border  white/10' : 'pointer  events  none'}
      `}
    >

 <div
     
        className={`flex justify  between items  center px  4 pt  2 xl:px  16 xl:pt  4 pb  2 h  16
        ${showHeader ? 'pt  [50px] pb  6' : 'pt  0'}
      `}>
        <img src="/logo.png" className="object  cover w  20 xl:w  22" />


        {/* Mobile Button */}
        <button
          className="z  20 w  10 h  10 relative xl:hidden"
         
       
          onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)

          }
        >
          <span className={`absolute hidden top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? 'rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          <span className={`absolute top  [16px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  opacity duration  300 ${isOpen ? 'opacity  0   translate  x  1/2' : 'opacity  100   translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          <span className={`absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? '  rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
        </button>


        {/* Desktop Menu */}
        <nav className="hidden xl:flex space  x  8 text  white font  semibold">
          <div className="relative group">
            <motion.a whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }} transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300 }} className="cursor  pointer hover:font  bold">About</motion.a>
            <div className="h  full">
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg
                opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0
                transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500
              ">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">History</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Vision</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Leadership</a>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>


          <div className="relative group">
            <span className="cursor  pointer">Residences</span>
            <div className="h  full">
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg
                opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0
                transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500
              ">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Floor</a>

                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Gallery</a>

          <a href="https://masterisehomes.com/lien  he" className="hover:text  amber  300">Contact</a>
        </nav>
      </div>


      {/* Mobile Sidebar */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {isOpen && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ x: '100%' }}
            animate={{ x: 0 }}
            exit={{ x: '100%' }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.5, ease: 'easeInOut' }}
            className="fixed top  0 right  0 h  full w  72 bg  gray  700 text  white p  6 shadow  lg space  y  4 opacity  [.90] xl:hidden"
          >


         
  <div className="sticky top  0 z  30 pl  40 pt  20 bg  gray  700">
       
       {!isTop && (
        <button
          className="z  20 w  10 h  10 static xl:hidden"
          onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)

          }
        >
          <span className={`absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? 'rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />

        </button>

)}


     <h1 className="text  2xl font  bold mb  6 mt  16">Menu</h1>
            <div className="space  y  6">

import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer  motion'


export default function Navbar({ onSidebarToggle }) {

```jsx
export default function Navbar() {

  return (

          {/* Mobile Button */}
          <button
            className="z  50 w  10 h  10 relative xl:hidden"
            onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
          >
            <span className={`absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? 'rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
            <span className={`absolute top  [16px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  opacity duration  300 ${isOpen ? 'opacity  0   translate  x  1/2' : 'opacity  100   translate  x  1/2'}`} />
            <span className={`absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? '  rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          </button>

          {/* Desktop Menu */}
          <nav className="hidden xl:flex space  x  8 text  white font  semibold">
            <div className="relative group">
              <motion.a whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }} transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300 }} className="cursor  pointer hover:font  bold">About</motion.a>
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg
                opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0
                transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">History</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Vision</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Leadership</a>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="relative group">
              <span className="cursor  pointer">Residences</span>
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg
                opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0
                transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Floor</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Plans</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Gallery</a>
              </div>
            </div>

            <a href="#location" className="hover:text  amber  300">Location</a>
            <a href="https://masterisehomes.com/lien  he" className="hover:text  amber  300">Contact</a>
          </nav>
        </div>
      </motion.header>

      <AnimatePresence>
        {isOpen && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ x: '100%' }}
            animate={{ x: 0 }}
            exit={{ x: '100%' }}

            className="fixed top  0 right  0 h  full w  72 bg  gray  700 text  white p  6 shadow  lg space  y  4 opacity  [.95] xl:hidden z  40"
          >
            <div className="sticky top  0 z  50 pt  4 bg  gray  700">
              <button
                onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
                className="w  10 h  10 relative"
              >
                <span className="absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]" />
                <span className="absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200   rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]" />
              </button>
            </div>
```

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer  motion'


export default function Navbar({onSidebarToggle}) {


  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false)
  const [showHeader, setShowHeader] = useState(false)


 
  useEffect(() => {
    onSidebarToggle?.(isOpen)
  }, [isOpen, onSidebarToggle])




  useEffect(() => {
    const handleScroll = () => {
      const scrollY = window.scrollY
      setShowHeader(scrollY > 1)
    }


    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
    return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
  }, [])


  return (
    <main>
      <motion.header
        animate={{ y: isOpen || showHeader ? 0 :   100 }}
        transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
        className="fixed top  0 left  0 z  50 w  full xl:pt  5 bg  black/40 shadow  md border  b border  white/10"
      >
        <div className="flex justify  between items  center px  4 pt  2 xl:px  16 xl:pt  4 pb  2 h  16">
          <img src="/logo.png" className="object  cover w  20 xl:w  22" />


          {/* Mobile Button */}
          <button
            className="z  50 w  10 h  10 relative xl:hidden"
            onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
          >
            <span className={`absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? 'rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
            <span className={`absolute top  [16px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  opacity duration  300 ${isOpen ? 'opacity  0   translate  x  1/2' : 'opacity  100   translate  x  1/2'}`} />
            <span className={`absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? '  rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          </button>

                {/* Mobile Sidebar */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {isOpen && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ x: '100%' }}
            animate={{ x: 0 }}
            exit={{ x: '100%' }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.5, ease: 'easeInOut' }}
            className="fixed top  0 right  0 h  full w  72 bg  gray  700 text  white p  6 shadow  lg space  y  4 opacity  [.95] xl:hidden z  40"
          >
            <div className="sticky top  0 z  50 pt  4 bg  gray  700">
              <button
                onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
                className="w  10 h  10 relative"
              >
                <span className="absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]" />
                <span className="absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200   rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]" />
              </button>
            </div>


            <h1 className="text  2xl font  bold mb  6 mt  8">Menu</h1>
            <div className="space  y  6">
              <div>
                <p className="font  bold">About</p>
                <ul className="pl  3 pt  2 text  sm text  gray  300 space  y  1">
                  <li>History</li>
                  <li>Vision</li>
                  <li>Leadership</li>
                </ul>
              </div>

```jsx
export default function Navbar({ onSidebarToggle }) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false)
  const [showHeader, setShowHeader] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => {
    onSidebarToggle?.(isOpen)
  }, [isOpen, onSidebarToggle])

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleScroll = () => {
      const scrollY = window.scrollY
      setShowHeader(scrollY > 1)
    }
    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
    return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
  }, [])

  return (
    <motion.header
      initial={false}
      animate={{ y: isOpen || showHeader ? 0 :   100 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
      className="fixed top  0 left  0 z  50 w  full bg  black/40 shadow  md border  b border  white/10"

      <div className="flex justify  between items  center px  4 pt  2 xl:px  16 xl:pt  4 pb  2 h  20">
        <img src="/logo.png" className="object  cover w  20 xl:w  22" />

        <button
          className="z  50 w  10 h  10 relative xl:hidden"
          onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
        >
          {/* Icon bars */}
        </button>

        {/* Menu desktop... */}
      </div>

      {/* Sidebar mobile */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {isOpen && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ x: '100%' }}
            animate={{ x: 0 }}
            exit={{ x: '100%' }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.4, ease: 'easeInOut' }}
            className="fixed top  0 right  0 h  full w  72 bg  gray  700 text  white p  6 shadow  lg opacity  95 xl:hidden z  40"
          >
            <button
              onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
              className="absolute top  5 right  5 w  10 h  10"
            >
              {/* Close icon */}
            </button>

            {/* Sidebar ná»™i dung */}
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </motion.header>
  )
}
```

```jsx
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer  motion'

export default function Navbar({ onSidebarToggle }) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false)
  const [showHeader, setShowHeader] = useState(false)

  useEffect(() => {
    onSidebarToggle?.(isOpen)
    // prevent scroll when menu open
    document.body.style.overflow = isOpen ? 'hidden' : 'auto'
    return () => {
      document.body.style.overflow = 'auto'
    }
  }, [isOpen, onSidebarToggle])

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleScroll = () => {
      const scrollY = window.scrollY
      setShowHeader(scrollY > 1)
    }

    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
    return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
  }, [])

  return (
    <main>
      <motion.header
        animate={{ y: isOpen || showHeader ? 0 :   100 }}
        transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
        className="fixed top  0 left  0 z  50 w  full xl:pt  5 bg  black/40 shadow  md border  b border  white/10"
      >
        <div className="flex justify  between items  center px  4 pt  2 xl:px  16 xl:pt  4 pb  2 h  16">
          <img src="/logo.png" className="object  cover w  20 xl:w  22" />

          {/* Mobile Button */}
          <button
            className="z  50 w  10 h  10 relative xl:hidden"
            onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
          >
            <span className={`absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? 'rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
            <span className={`absolute top  [16px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  opacity duration  300 ${isOpen ? 'opacity  0   translate  x  1/2' : 'opacity  100   translate  x  1/2'}`} />
            <span className={`absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? '  rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          </button>

          {/* Desktop Menu */}
          <nav className="hidden xl:flex space  x  8 text  white font  semibold">
            <div className="relative group">
              <motion.a whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }} transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300 }} className="cursor  pointer hover:font  bold">About</motion.a>
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0 transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">History</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Vision</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Leadership</a>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="relative group">
              <span className="cursor  pointer">Residences</span>
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0 transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Floor</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Plans</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Gallery</a>
              </div>
            </div>
            <a href="#location" className="hover:text  amber  300">Location</a>
            <a href="https://masterisehomes.com/lien  he" className="hover:text  amber  300">Contact</a>
          </nav>
        </div>
      </motion.header>

      {/* Mobile Sidebar */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {isOpen && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ x: '100%' }}
            animate={{ x: 0 }}
            exit={{ x: '100%' }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.5, ease: 'easeInOut' }}
            className="fixed top  0 right  0 h  full w  72 bg  gray  700 text  white p  6 shadow  lg space  y  4 opacity  [.95] xl:hidden z  40"
          >
            <div className="sticky top  0 z  50 pt  4 bg  gray  700">
              <button
                onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
                className="w  10 h  10 relative"
              >
                <span className="absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]" />
                <span className="absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200   rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]" />
              </button>
            </div>
            <h1 className="text  2xl font  bold mb  6 mt  8">Menu</h1>
            <div className="space  y  6">
              <div>
                <p className="font  bold">About</p>
                <ul className="pl  3 pt  2 text  sm text  gray  300 space  y  1">
                  <li>History</li>
                  <li>Vision</li>
                  <li>Leadership</li>
                </ul>
              </div>
              <div>

                <ul className="pl  3 pt  2 text  sm text  gray  300 space  y  1">
                  <li>Floor Plans</li>
                  <li>Amenities</li>
                  <li>Gallery</li>
                </ul>
              </div>
              <a className="block font  bold">Location</a>
              <a className="block font  bold">Contact</a>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </main>
  )
}
```

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer  motion'


export default function Navbar({ onSidebarToggle }) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false)
  const [showHeader, setShowHeader] = useState(false)


useEffect(() => {
  onSidebarToggle?.(isOpen)
  document.body.style.overflow = isOpen ? 'hidden' : 'auto'
  return () => {
    document.body.style.overflow = 'auto'
  }
}, [isOpen, onSidebarToggle])




useEffect(() => {
  const handleScroll = () => {
    const scrollY = window.scrollY
    setShowHeader(scrollY > 1)
  }


  window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
  return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
}, [])


  return (
    <main>
    <motion.header
  initial={{ y:   100 }}
  animate={{ y: isOpen ? 0 : (showHeader ? 0 :   100) }}
  transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
  className="fixed top  0 left  0 z  50 w  full bg  black/40 shadow  md border  b border  white/10"
>

        <div className="flex justify  between items  center px  4 pt  2 xl:px  16 xl:pt  4 pb  2 h  16">
          <img src="/logo.png" className="object  cover w  20 xl:w  22" />


          {/* Mobile Button */}
          <button
            className="z  50 w  10 h  10 relative xl:hidden"
            onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
          >
            <span className={`absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? 'rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
            <span className={`absolute top  [16px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  opacity duration  300 ${isOpen ? 'opacity  0   translate  x  1/2' : 'opacity  100   translate  x  1/2'}`} />
            <span className={`absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 transition  all duration  300 origin  center ${isOpen ? '  rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]' : '  translate  x  1/2'}`} />
          </button>


          {/* Desktop Menu */}
          <nav className="hidden xl:flex space  x  8 text  white font  semibold">
            <div className="relative group">
              <motion.a whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }} transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300 }} className="cursor  pointer hover:font  bold">About</motion.a>
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0 transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">History</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Vision</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Leadership</a>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="relative group">
              <span className="cursor  pointer">Residences</span>
              <div className="desktop absolute left  0 bg  amber  50 text  base p  6 pb  10 pt  5 mt  5 space  y  2 rounded shadow  lg opacity  0 translate  y  12 group  hover:opacity  100 group  hover:translate  y  0 transition  all duration  700 ease  in  out pointer  events  none group  hover:pointer  events  auto border  sky  500">
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Floor</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Plans</a>
                <a className="text  amber  300 hover:text  amber  400">Gallery</a>
              </div>
            </div>
            <a href="#location" className="hover:text  amber  300">Location</a>
            <a href="https://masterisehomes.com/lien  he" className="hover:text  amber  300">Contact</a>
          </nav>
        </div>
      </motion.header>


      {/* Mobile Sidebar */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {isOpen && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ x: '100%' }}
            animate={{ x: 0 }}
            exit={{ x: '100%' }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.5, ease: 'easeInOut' }}
            className="fixed top  0 right  0 h  full w  72 bg  gray  700 text  white p  6 shadow  lg space  y  4 opacity  [.95] xl:hidden z  40"
          >
            <div className="sticky top  0 z  50 pt  4 bg  gray  700">
              <button
                onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
                className="w  10 h  10 relative"
              >
                <span className="absolute top  [8px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200 rotate  45   translate  x  1/2 translate  y  [8px]" />
                <span className="absolute top  [24px] left  1/2 w  [24px] h  [2px] bg  sky  200   rotate  45   translate  x  1/2   translate  y  [8px]" />
              </button>
            </div>
            <h1 className="text  2xl font  bold mb  6 mt  8">Menu</h1>
            <div className="space  y  6">
              <div>
                <p className="font  bold">About</p>
                <ul className="pl  3 pt  2 text  sm text  gray  300 space  y  1">
                  <li>History</li>
                  <li>Vision</li>
                  <li>Leadership</li>
                </ul>
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="font  bold">Residences</p>
                <ul className="pl  3 pt  2 text  sm text  gray  300 space  y  1">
                  <li>Floor Plans</li>
                  <li>Amenities</li>
                  <li>Gallery</li>
                </ul>
              </div>
              <a className="block font  bold">Location</a>
              <a className="block font  bold">Contact</a>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </main>
  )
}
